```{.python .input  n=2}
index = 'r14_01_14a'
cache_path = '/home/aaron/lab/local/processed/' + index + '.hdf5'
cache_path = g.default_processed + index + '.hdf5'

r = g.ProcessedRun(cache_path=cache_path)

u_levels = np.linspace(*np.percentile(r.Uf[...], (1, 99)), num=100)

tf = r.Tf[:, 0, :]
zf = r.Zf[:, 0, :]
```

```{.python .input  n=3}
def bandpass(signal, cutoff, high_cutoff=False, axis=-1):
    fft = np.fft.rfft(signal, axis=axis)
    freqs = np.fft.rfftfreq(signal.shape[axis], d=0.01)
    
    s = [slice(None) for _ in range(signal.ndim)]
    s[axis] = freqs < cutoff
    rfft = fft.copy()
    rfft[s] = 0
    
    if high_cutoff:
        s[axis] = freqs > high_cutoff
        rfft[s] = 0
        
    rdata = np.fft.irfft(rfft)
    return rdata
```

```{.python .input  n=4}
where = np.s_[10, 10, :3000]

u1 = bandpass(r.U[where], 0.21, 0.35)
v1 = bandpass(r.V[where], 0.21, 0.35)
w1 = bandpass(r.W[where], 0.21, 0.35)

w = (u1 ** 2 + v1 ** 2 + w1 ** 2) ** .5
u = (u1 ** 2 + v1 ** 2 + w1 ** 2) ** .5

plt.figure()
plt.plot(r.U[where])
plt.plot(u)
plt.plot(u1)

plt.figure()
plt.plot(r.W[where])
plt.plot(w)
plt.plot(w1)

plt.figure()
plt.plot(u1)
plt.plot(v1)
plt.plot(w1)
plt.axhline(0)
plt.ylim(-0.001, 0.001)
```

```{.python .input  n=5}
def v(a, g):
    sa = np.sin(a)[None].T
    ca = np.cos(a)[None].T
    sg = np.sin(g)[None].T
    cg = np.cos(g)[None].T
    
    return (-u1 * sa * cg) + (v1 * ca * cg) + (w1 * sg)

def u(a, g):
    sa = np.sin(a)[None].T
    ca = np.cos(a)[None].T
    sg = np.sin(g)[None].T
    cg = np.cos(g)[None].T
    
    return u1 * ca + v1 * sa

def w(a, g):
    sa = np.sin(a)[None].T
    ca = np.cos(a)[None].T
    sg = np.sin(g)[None].T
    cg = np.cos(g)[None].T
    
    return u1 * sa * sg - v1 * ca * sg + w1 * cg
    
a = np.linspace(-0.3, 0.3, 100)
g = np.linspace(-0.4, 0.4, 200)

A, G = np.meshgrid(a, g)

def f((A, G), axis=None):
    return np.linalg.norm(v(A, G), axis=axis)

plt.contourf(A, G, f((A, G), axis=2).T, 100)
plt.colorbar()

import scipy.optimize as opt

minim = opt.minimize(f, [0, 0])
print minim.x
```

```{.python .input  n=485}
all = np.s_[10, 10, :]

def v(a, g):
    sa = np.sin(a)[None].T
    ca = np.cos(a)[None].T
    sg = np.sin(g)[None].T
    cg = np.cos(g)[None].T
    
    return (-r.U[all] * sa * cg) + (r.V[all] * ca * cg) + (r.W[all] * sg)

mv = v(A, G).mean(axis=-1) ** 2


```

```{.python .input  n=13}
umag = (u1 ** 2 + v1 ** 2 + w1 ** 2) ** .5

wr = -np.sign(u1) * umag / (1 + uwr ** 2) ** .5  # approx, because u1 ~= u
ur = wr * uwr

plt.figure()
plt.plot(u1)
plt.plot(ur)

plt.figure()
plt.plot(w1)
plt.plot(wr)

plt.figure()
plt.plot(v1)
plt.plot(vr)
```

```{.python .input  n=12}
def kabsch(vec, vecr):
    # now do least squares minimisation through SVD to find the rotation
    # matrix R, vecr = R vec
    
    # covariance matrix
    C = np.dot(vec, vecr.T)
    
    # svd of the covariance matrix
    V, S, Wh = np.linalg.svd(C)

    d = np.sign(np.linalg.det(V.T) * np.linalg.det(Wh))
    
    corr = np.eye(3)
    corr[-1, -1] = d

    print V.T
    print
    print np.dot(corr, V.T)
    print
    print np.array([1, 1, d])[None] * V.T
    
    
    R = np.dot(Wh.T, np.dot(corr, V.T))
    return R

vec = np.vstack((u1, v1, w1))
vecr = np.vstack((ur, np.zeros(ur.size), wr))
R = kabsch(vec, vecr)
```

```{.python .input  n=39}
bsu = bandpass(r.U[:, :, :3000].mean(axis=1), 0.1, 0.65)
plt.contourf(bsu, 100)
plt.colorbar()

plt.figure()
plt.plot(np.abs(bsu).mean(axis=1) / np.abs(bsu[-1]).mean())
```

```{.python .input  n=40}
bsv = bandpass(r.V[:, :, :3000].mean(axis=1), 0.1, 0.65)
plt.contourf(bsv, 100)
plt.colorbar()

plt.figure()
plt.plot(np.abs(bsv).mean(axis=1) / np.abs(bsv[-1]).mean())
```

```{.python .input  n=41}
bsw = bandpass(r.W[:, :, :3000].mean(axis=1), 0.1, 0.65)
plt.contourf(bsw, 100)
plt.colorbar()

plt.figure()
vertical_w = np.abs(bsw).mean(axis=1) / np.abs(bsw[-1]).mean()
plt.plot(vertical_w)
```

```{.python .input  n=6}
u1 = r.U[-1, 50, :3000]
v1 = r.V[-1, 50, :3000]
w1 = r.W[-1, 50, :3000]


def u(a, g):
    sa = np.sin(a)[None].T
    ca = np.cos(a)[None].T
    sg = np.sin(g)[None].T
    cg = np.cos(g)[None].T
    
    return u1 * ca + v1 * sa

def v(a, g, u1=u1, v1=v1, w1=w1):
    sa = np.sin(a)[None].T
    ca = np.cos(a)[None].T
    sg = np.sin(g)[None].T
    cg = np.cos(g)[None].T
    
    return (-u1 * sa * cg) + (v1 * ca * cg) + (w1 * sg)


def w(a, g):
    sa = np.sin(a)[None].T
    ca = np.cos(a)[None].T
    sg = np.sin(g)[None].T
    cg = np.cos(g)[None].T
    
    return u1 * sa * sg - v1 * ca * sg + w1 * cg
    
a = np.linspace(-0.3, 0.3, 100)
g = np.linspace(-0.4, 0.4, 200)

A, G = np.meshgrid(a, g)

def f((A, G), axis=None):
    return np.linalg.norm(v(A, G), axis=axis)

plt.contourf(A, G, f((A, G), axis=2).T, 100)
plt.colorbar()

import scipy.optimize as opt

minim = opt.minimize(f, [0, 0])
print minim.x
```

```{.python .input  n=16}
u1 = bandpass(r.U[-1, 50, :3000], 0.2, 3)
v1 = bandpass(r.V[-1, 50, :3000], 0.2, 3)
w1 = bandpass(r.W[-1, 50, :3000], 0.2, 3)

# full 3d rotation
def v3(a, b, g, u1=u1, v1=v1, w1=w1):
    sa = np.sin(a)[None].T
    ca = np.cos(a)[None].T
    
    sb = np.sin(b)[None].T
    cb = np.cos(b)[None].T
    
    sg = np.sin(g)[None].T
    cg = np.cos(g)[None].T
    
    return -u1 * (sa * cg + ca * sb * cg) + v1 * (ca * cg - sa * sb * sg) + w1 * (cb * cg)
```

```{.python .input  n=47}
a = np.linspace(-0.3, 0.3, 100)
b = np.linspace(-0.3, 0.3, 100)
g = np.linspace(-0.4, 0.4, 100)

A3, B3, G3 = np.meshgrid(a, b, g, indexing='xy')

def f3((A, B, G), axis=None):
    return np.linalg.norm(v3(A, 0, 0), axis=axis)

import scipy.optimize as opt

minim3 = opt.minimize(f3, [0, 0, 0])
print np.rad2deg(minim3.x)
```

```{.json .output n=47}
 }

```

```{.python .input  n=37}
vf3 = f3((A3, B3, G3), axis=-1)
```

```{.python .input  n=39}
plt.contourf(vf3[:, :, 0], 100)
```
